name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted May 13, 2024
msg:I took my 90-year-old mother home from Sanya. I had to go to Huangshan on the way, so I stayed in Nanjing for two days to show my mother around. So I chose the Lakeside Jinling Hotel on Ctrip, which has a good review. It is close to Nanjing South High-speed Railway Station. When I entered the hotel yard, I was attracted by the pleasant garden scenery. It is divided into several two-story buildings. There is a garden corridor between the buildings. It is so beautiful. The hotel is right by Baijia Lake. You can see the lake view on the balcony. Although the hotel facilities are a bit old, the hygiene and service are definitely five-star standards. The hotel service staff is absolutely meticulous. It was Mother's Day. As soon as I entered the room, I was moved by the dolls made of bath towels and various small gifts. I was moved. Let's talk about the hotel's breakfast. It is mainly Chinese breakfast with rich varieties, especially Nanjing local snacks. A bowl of duck blood vermicelli is so delicious, and Xiaolongbao, etc., you can eat authentic snacks without leaving the hotel. The service of the restaurant is even better. My mother is 90 years old. As long as there are stairs, they will come to help the elderly. Is there a restaurant manager to ask what you need and how is the food? If you need anything, they will personally bring you coffee and tea. On the last day, when they heard that we were going to take the high-speed train, they immediately made us lattes in take-out paper cups so that we could take them on the road. This stay was really great. The environment, service, and dining were all very comfortable and fun. I will bring my mother to Nanjing in the fall and stay at the Lakeside Jinling Hotel. The service guy at the front desk was also very considerate and personally brought the luggage to the room.
